    <a id="3410" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3410" class="Generalizable">m</a> <a id="3412" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3412" class="Generalizable">n</a>     <a id="3418" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3420" href="Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#203" class="Datatype">ℕ</a>
    <a id="3426" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3426" class="Generalizable">S</a> <a id="3428" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3428" class="Generalizable">T</a> <a id="3430" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3430" class="Generalizable">U</a>   <a id="3434" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3436" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1064" class="Function">Subset</a> <a id="3443" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3412" class="Generalizable">n</a>
    <a id="3449" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3449" class="Generalizable">i</a> <a id="3451" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3451" class="Generalizable">j</a> <a id="3453" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3453" class="Generalizable">x</a> <a id="3455" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3455" class="Generalizable">y</a> <a id="3457" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3459" href="Data.Fin.Base.html#1154" class="Datatype">Fin</a> <a id="3463" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3412" class="Generalizable">n</a>

</pre>
Extensionally equal subsets are definitionally equal:

<pre class="Agda"><a id="extensionality"></a><a id="3560" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3560" class="Function">extensionality</a> <a id="3575" class="Symbol">:</a>
    <a id="3581" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="3583" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1584" class="Function Operator">_∈</a> <a id="3586" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3426" class="Generalizable">S</a><a id="3587" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3589" href="Relation.Unary.html#2330" class="Function Operator">≐</a> <a id="3591" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3592" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1584" class="Function Operator">_∈</a> <a id="3595" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3428" class="Generalizable">T</a><a id="3596" class="Symbol">))</a>
  <a id="3601" class="Symbol">→</a>      <a id="3608" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3426" class="Generalizable">S</a>  <a id="3611" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#150" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a>     <a id="3617" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3428" class="Generalizable">T</a>
<a id="3619" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3560" class="Function">extensionality</a> <a id="3634" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="3636" href="Data.Product.Base.html#3109" class="Function">uncurry</a> <a id="3644" href="Data.Fin.Subset.Properties.html#6292" class="Function">⊆-antisym</a>
</pre>
<pre class="Agda"><a id="_≟_"></a><a id="3667" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3667" class="Function Operator">_≟_</a> <a id="3671" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3673" href="Relation.Binary.Definitions.html#6469" class="Function">DecidableEquality</a> <a id="3691" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3692" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1064" class="Function">Subset</a> <a id="3699" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3412" class="Generalizable">n</a><a id="3700" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="3702" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3667" class="Function Operator">_≟_</a> <a id="3706" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="3708" href="Data.Vec.Properties.html#2011" class="Function">≡-dec</a> <a id="3714" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#595" class="Function Operator">_≟ᵇ_</a>
</pre>
We define disjointness of sets:

<pre class="Agda"><a id="Disjoint"></a><a id="3765" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3765" class="Function">Disjoint</a> <a id="3774" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3776" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1064" class="Function">Subset</a> <a id="3783" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3412" class="Generalizable">n</a> <a id="3785" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3787" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1064" class="Function">Subset</a> <a id="3794" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3412" class="Generalizable">n</a> <a id="3796" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3798" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">Set</a>
<a id="3802" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3765" class="Function">Disjoint</a> <a id="3811" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3811" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="3813" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3813" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="3815" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="3817" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#2783" class="Function">Empty</a> <a id="3823" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3824" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3811" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="3826" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#2126" class="Function Operator">∩</a> <a id="3828" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3813" class="Bound">T</a><a id="3829" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="Disjoint-as-≡"></a><a id="3832" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3832" class="Function">Disjoint-as-≡</a> <a id="3846" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3848" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3765" class="Function">Disjoint</a> <a id="3857" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3426" class="Generalizable">S</a> <a id="3859" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3428" class="Generalizable">T</a> <a id="3861" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3863" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3426" class="Generalizable">S</a> <a id="3865" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#2126" class="Function Operator">∩</a> <a id="3867" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3428" class="Generalizable">T</a> <a id="3869" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#150" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="3871" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#883" class="Function">∅</a>
<a id="3873" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3832" class="Function">Disjoint-as-≡</a> <a id="3887" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="3889" href="Data.Fin.Subset.Properties.html#3967" class="Function">Empty-unique</a>

    <a id="8486" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="8491" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8492" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8492" class="Bound">y∈⁅x⁆∪S</a> <a id="8500" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#235" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="8502" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8502" class="Bound">y≢x</a><a id="8505" class="Symbol">)</a> ← <a id="8509" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8149" class="Function">x∈S-y⇒x∈S×x≢y</a> <a id="8523" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8470" class="Bound">y∈[⁅x⁆∪S]-x</a>
    <a id="8539" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="8544" href="Data.Fin.Subset.Properties.html#21037" class="Function">x∈p∪q⁻</a> <a id="8551" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="8553" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="8555" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8492" class="Bound">y∈⁅x⁆∪S</a>
  <a id="8565" class="Symbol">...</a>  <a id="8570" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="8572" href="Data.Sum.Base.html#675" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₁</a> <a id="8577" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8577" class="Bound">y∈⁅x⁆</a> <a id="8583" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8585" href="Relation.Nullary.Negation.Core.html#1226" class="Function">contradiction</a> <a id="8599" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8600" href="Data.Fin.Subset.Properties.html#5441" class="Function">x∈⁅y⁆⇒x≡y</a> <a id="8610" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="8612" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8577" class="Bound">y∈⁅x⁆</a><a id="8617" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8619" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8502" class="Bound">y≢x</a>
  <a id="8625" class="Symbol">...</a>  <a id="8630" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="8632" href="Data.Sum.Base.html#700" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₂</a> <a id="8637" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8637" class="Bound">y∈S</a>   <a id="8643" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8645" href="Data.Fin.Subset.Properties.html#24414" class="Function">x∈p∧x≢y⇒x∈p-y</a> <a id="8659" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8637" class="Bound">y∈S</a> <a id="8663" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8502" class="Bound">y≢x</a>

  <a id="8670" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8670" class="Function">S-x⊆[⁅x⁆∪S]-x</a> <a id="8684" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8686" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8351" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="8688" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#2524" class="Function Operator">-</a> <a id="8690" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8353" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="8692" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1686" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="8694" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8695" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1365" class="Function Operator">⁅</a> <a id="8697" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8353" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="8699" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1365" class="Function Operator">⁆</a> <a id="8701" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#2181" class="Function Operator">∪</a> <a id="8703" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8351" class="Bound">S</a><a id="8704" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8706" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#2524" class="Function Operator">-</a> <a id="8708" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8353" class="Bound">x</a>
  <a id="8712" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8670" class="Function">S-x⊆[⁅x⁆∪S]-x</a> <a id="8726" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8726" class="Bound">y∈S-x</a>
    <a id="8736" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="8741" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8742" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8742" class="Bound">x∈S</a> <a id="8746" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#235" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="8748" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8748" class="Bound">x≢y</a><a id="8751" class="Symbol">)</a> ← <a id="8755" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8149" class="Function">x∈S-y⇒x∈S×x≢y</a> <a id="8769" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8726" class="Bound">y∈S-x</a>
    <a id="8779" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8781" href="Data.Fin.Subset.Properties.html#24414" class="Function">x∈p∧x≢y⇒x∈p-y</a> <a id="8795" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8796" href="Data.Fin.Subset.Properties.html#21309" class="Function">x∈p∪q⁺</a> <a id="8803" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8804" href="Data.Sum.Base.html#700" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₂</a> <a id="8809" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8742" class="Bound">x∈S</a><a id="8812" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="8815" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8748" class="Bound">x≢y</a>

<a id="x∉S⇒S-x≡S"></a><a id="8820" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8820" class="Function">x∉S⇒S-x≡S</a> <a id="8830" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8832" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3453" class="Generalizable">x</a> <a id="8834" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1638" class="Function Operator">∉</a> <a id="8836" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3426" class="Generalizable">S</a> <a id="8838" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8840" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3426" class="Generalizable">S</a> <a id="8842" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#2524" class="Function Operator">-</a> <a id="8844" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3453" class="Generalizable">x</a> <a id="8846" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#150" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="8848" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3426" class="Generalizable">S</a>
<a id="8850" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8820" class="Function">x∉S⇒S-x≡S</a> <a id="8860" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8861" class="Argument">x</a> <a id="8863" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8865" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8865" class="Bound">x</a><a id="8866" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8868" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8869" class="Argument">S</a> <a id="8871" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8873" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8873" class="Bound">S</a><a id="8874" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8876" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8876" class="Bound">x∉S</a> <a id="8880" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8882" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3560" class="Function">extensionality</a> <a id="8897" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8898" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8923" class="Function">S-x⊆S</a> <a id="8904" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#235" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="8906" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8973" class="Function">S⊆S-x</a><a id="8911" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="8915" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="8923" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8923" class="Function">S-x⊆S</a> <a id="8929" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8931" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8873" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="8933" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#2524" class="Function Operator">-</a> <a id="8935" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8865" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="8937" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1686" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="8939" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8873" class="Bound">S</a>
  <a id="8943" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8923" class="Function">S-x⊆S</a> <a id="8949" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8951" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#2226" class="Field Operator">_₁</a> <a id="8954" href="Function.Base.html#1115" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="8956" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8149" class="Function">x∈S-y⇒x∈S×x≢y</a>

  <a id="8973" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8973" class="Function">S⊆S-x</a> <a id="8979" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8981" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8873" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="8983" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1686" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="8985" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8873" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="8987" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#2524" class="Function Operator">-</a> <a id="8989" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8865" class="Bound">x</a>
  <a id="8993" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8973" class="Function">S⊆S-x</a> <a id="8999" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8999" class="Bound">y∈S</a> <a id="9003" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9005" href="Data.Fin.Subset.Properties.html#24414" class="Function">x∈p∧x≢y⇒x∈p-y</a> <a id="9019" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8999" class="Bound">y∈S</a> <a id="9023" class="Symbol">λ{</a> <a id="9026" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#207" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="9031" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9033" href="Relation.Nullary.Negation.Core.html#1226" class="Function">contradiction</a> <a id="9047" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8999" class="Bound">y∈S</a> <a id="9051" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#8876" class="Bound">x∉S</a> <a id="9055" class="Symbol">}</a>
</pre>
We define a more ergonomic form of strong induction:

<pre class="Agda"><a id="9124" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="9131" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9131" class="Module">_</a> <a id="9133" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9134" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9134" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="9136" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9138" href="Relation.Unary.html#1232" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="9143" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9144" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1064" class="Function">Subset</a> <a id="9151" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3412" class="Generalizable">n</a><a id="9152" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9154" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3390" class="Generalizable">a</a><a id="9155" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="9159" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9160" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9160" class="Bound">P-∅</a> <a id="9164" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9166" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9134" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="9168" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#883" class="Function">∅</a><a id="9169" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="9173" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9174" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9174" class="Bound">P-ind</a> <a id="9180" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9182" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="9184" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9185" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9185" class="Bound">S</a><a id="9186" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9188" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9190" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#2721" class="Function">Nonempty</a> <a id="9199" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9185" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="9201" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9203" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9204" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1800" class="Function Operator">_⊂</a> <a id="9207" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9185" class="Bound">S</a><a id="9208" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9210" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3360" class="Function Operator">⊆ᴾ</a> <a id="9213" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9134" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="9215" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9217" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9134" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="9219" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9185" class="Bound">S</a><a id="9220" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="9224" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="9232" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="9237" href="Induction.WellFounded.html#2991" class="Module">Wf.All</a> <a id="9244" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9245" href="Data.Fin.Subset.Induction.html#947" class="Function">⊂-wellFounded</a> <a id="9259" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9260" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9151" class="Bound">n</a><a id="9261" class="Symbol">})</a> <a id="9264" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="9270" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9271" href="Induction.WellFounded.html#3153" class="Function">wfRec</a><a id="9276" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="9280" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="9285" href="Relation.Unary.html" class="Module">Relation.Unary</a> <a id="9300" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="9306" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9307" href="Relation.Unary.html#2539" class="Function Operator">_⊆′_</a><a id="9311" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="9316" class="Keyword">private</a>
    <a id="9328" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9328" class="Function">step</a> <a id="9333" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9335" href="Induction.WellFounded.html#1148" class="Function">Wf.WfRec</a> <a id="9344" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1800" class="Function Operator">_⊂_</a> <a id="9348" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9134" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="9350" href="Relation.Unary.html#2539" class="Function Operator">⊆′</a> <a id="9353" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9134" class="Bound">P</a>
    <a id="9359" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9328" class="Function">step</a> <a id="9364" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9364" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="9366" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9366" class="Bound">P-ind-⊂</a>
      <a id="9380" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="9385" href="Data.Fin.Subset.Properties.html#4201" class="Function">nonempty?</a> <a id="9395" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9364" class="Bound">S</a>
    <a id="9401" class="Symbol">...</a>  <a id="9406" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="9408" href="Relation.Nullary.Decidable.Core.html#1655" class="InductiveConstructor">no</a>  <a id="9412" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9412" class="Bound">Empty-S</a> <a id="9420" class="Keyword">rewrite</a> <a id="9428" href="Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#1712" class="Function">Eq.sym</a> <a id="9435" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9436" href="Data.Fin.Subset.Properties.html#3967" class="Function">Empty-unique</a> <a id="9449" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9412" class="Bound">Empty-S</a><a id="9456" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9458" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9460" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9160" class="Bound">P-∅</a>
    <a id="9468" class="Symbol">...</a>  <a id="9473" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="9475" href="Relation.Nullary.Decidable.Core.html#1618" class="InductiveConstructor">yes</a> <a id="9479" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9479" class="Bound">Nonempty-S</a> <a id="9490" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9492" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9174" class="Bound">P-ind</a> <a id="9498" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9479" class="Bound">Nonempty-S</a> <a id="9509" class="Bound">P-ind-⊂</a>

  <a id="9520" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9520" class="Function">strong-induction</a> <a id="9537" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9539" href="Relation.Unary.html#3491" class="Function">Π[</a> <a id="9542" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9134" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="9544" href="Relation.Unary.html#3491" class="Function">]</a>
  <a id="9548" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9520" class="Function">strong-induction</a> <a id="9565" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9567" href="Induction.WellFounded.html#3153" class="Function">wfRec</a> <a id="9573" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="9575" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="9577" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9328" class="Function">step</a>
</pre>
For convenience, we define a version of strong induction that provides an explicit element of the set:

<pre class="Agda"><a id="9699" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="9706" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9706" class="Module">_</a> <a id="9708" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9709" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9709" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="9711" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9713" href="Relation.Unary.html#1232" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="9718" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9719" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1064" class="Function">Subset</a> <a id="9726" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3412" class="Generalizable">n</a><a id="9727" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9729" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3390" class="Generalizable">a</a><a id="9730" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="9734" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9735" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9735" class="Bound">P-∅</a> <a id="9739" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9741" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9709" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="9743" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#883" class="Function">∅</a><a id="9744" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="9748" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9749" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9749" class="Bound">P-ind</a> <a id="9755" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9757" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="9759" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9760" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9760" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="9762" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9762" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9763" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9765" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9767" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9768" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1800" class="Function Operator">_⊂</a> <a id="9771" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9772" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1365" class="Function Operator">⁅</a> <a id="9774" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9762" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="9776" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1365" class="Function Operator">⁆</a> <a id="9778" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#2181" class="Function Operator">∪</a> <a id="9780" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9760" class="Bound">S</a><a id="9781" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="9784" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3360" class="Function Operator">⊆ᴾ</a> <a id="9787" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9709" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="9789" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9791" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9762" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="9793" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1638" class="Function Operator">∉</a> <a id="9795" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9760" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="9797" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9799" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9709" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="9801" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9802" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1365" class="Function Operator">⁅</a> <a id="9804" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9762" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="9806" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1365" class="Function Operator">⁆</a> <a id="9808" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#2181" class="Function Operator">∪</a> <a id="9810" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9760" class="Bound">S</a><a id="9811" class="Symbol">))</a>
  <a id="9816" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="9824" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="9829" href="Induction.WellFounded.html#2991" class="Module">Wf.All</a> <a id="9836" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9837" href="Data.Fin.Subset.Induction.html#947" class="Function">⊂-wellFounded</a> <a id="9851" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9852" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9726" class="Bound">n</a><a id="9853" class="Symbol">})</a> <a id="9856" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="9862" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9863" href="Induction.WellFounded.html#3153" class="Function">wfRec</a><a id="9868" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="9872" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="9877" href="Relation.Unary.html" class="Module">Relation.Unary</a> <a id="9892" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="9898" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9899" href="Relation.Unary.html#2539" class="Function Operator">_⊆′_</a><a id="9903" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="9908" class="Keyword">private</a>
    <a id="9920" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9920" class="Function">step</a> <a id="9925" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9927" href="Induction.WellFounded.html#1148" class="Function">Wf.WfRec</a> <a id="9936" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1800" class="Function Operator">_⊂_</a> <a id="9940" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9709" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="9942" href="Relation.Unary.html#2539" class="Function Operator">⊆′</a> <a id="9945" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9709" class="Bound">P</a>
    <a id="9951" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9920" class="Function">step</a> <a id="9956" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9956" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="9958" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9958" class="Bound">P-ind-⊂S</a>
      <a id="9973" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="9978" href="Data.Fin.Subset.Properties.html#4201" class="Function">nonempty?</a> <a id="9988" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9956" class="Bound">S</a>
    <a id="9994" class="Symbol">...</a>  <a id="9999" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="10001" href="Relation.Nullary.Decidable.Core.html#1655" class="InductiveConstructor">no</a>  <a id="10005" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#10005" class="Bound">Empty-S</a> <a id="10013" class="Keyword">rewrite</a> <a id="10021" href="Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#1712" class="Function">Eq.sym</a> <a id="10028" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10029" href="Data.Fin.Subset.Properties.html#3967" class="Function">Empty-unique</a> <a id="10042" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#10005" class="Bound">Empty-S</a><a id="10049" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10051" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10053" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9735" class="Bound">P-∅</a>
    <a id="10061" class="Symbol">...</a>  <a id="10066" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="10068" href="Relation.Nullary.Decidable.Core.html#1618" class="InductiveConstructor">yes</a> <a id="10072" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10073" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#10073" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="10075" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#235" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="10077" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#10077" class="Bound">x∈S</a><a id="10080" class="Symbol">)</a>
           <a id="10093" class="Keyword">rewrite</a> <a id="10101" href="Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#1712" class="Function">Eq.sym</a> <a id="10108" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10109" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#7310" class="Function">x∈S⇒⁅x⁆∪[S-x]≡S</a> <a id="10125" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#10077" class="Bound">x∈S</a><a id="10128" class="Symbol">)</a>
           <a id="10141" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10143" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9749" class="Bound">P-ind</a> <a id="10149" class="Bound">P-ind-⊂S</a> <a id="10158" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10159" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#7963" class="Function">x∉S-x</a> <a id="10165" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="10167" class="Symbol">_)</a>

  <a id="10173" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#10173" class="Function">pointed-strong-induction</a> <a id="10198" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10200" href="Relation.Unary.html#3491" class="Function">Π[</a> <a id="10203" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9709" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="10205" href="Relation.Unary.html#3491" class="Function">]</a>
  <a id="10209" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#10173" class="Function">pointed-strong-induction</a> <a id="10234" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10236" href="Induction.WellFounded.html#3153" class="Function">wfRec</a> <a id="10242" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="10244" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="10246" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#9920" class="Function">step</a>
</pre>
We define induction on the elements of a subset:

<pre class="Agda"><a id="10314" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="10321" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#10321" class="Module">_</a> <a id="10323" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10324" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#10324" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="10326" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10328" href="Relation.Unary.html#1232" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="10333" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10334" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1064" class="Function">Subset</a> <a id="10341" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3412" class="Generalizable">n</a><a id="10342" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10344" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3390" class="Generalizable">a</a><a id="10345" class="Symbol">}</a>

      <a id="13015" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#13015" class="Function">x∉T</a> <a id="13019" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13021" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#12387" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="13023" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1638" class="Function Operator">∉</a> <a id="13025" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#12402" class="Bound">T</a>
      <a id="13033" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#13015" class="Function">x∉T</a> <a id="13037" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13039" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#11029" class="Function">Disjoint⁅x⁆⇒x∉</a> <a id="13054" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13055" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#4235" class="Function">Disjoint-∪⁻</a> <a id="13067" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#12404" class="Bound">Disjoint-⁅x⁆∪S-T</a><a id="13083" class="Symbol">)</a>

      <a id="13092" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#13092" class="Function">Disjoint-S-⁅x⁆∪T</a> <a id="13109" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13111" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3765" class="Function">Disjoint</a> <a id="13120" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#12391" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="13122" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13123" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1365" class="Function Operator">⁅</a> <a id="13125" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#12387" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="13127" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1365" class="Function Operator">⁆</a> <a id="13129" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#2181" class="Function Operator">∪</a> <a id="13131" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#12402" class="Bound">T</a><a id="13132" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="13140" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#13092" class="Function">Disjoint-S-⁅x⁆∪T</a> <a id="13157" class="Symbol">=</a>
        <a id="13167" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#4792" class="Function">Disjoint-swap</a>
          <a id="13191" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13192" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3903" class="Function">Disjoint-sym</a> <a id="13205" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13206" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#10875" class="Function">x∉⇒Disjoint⁅x⁆</a> <a id="13221" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#12394" class="Bound">x∉S</a><a id="13224" class="Symbol">))</a>
          <a id="13237" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13238" href="Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#1808" class="Function">Eq.subst</a> <a id="13247" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="13250" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#13250" class="Bound">∙</a> <a id="13252" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13254" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3765" class="Function">Disjoint</a> <a id="13263" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#13250" class="Bound">∙</a> <a id="13265" class="Symbol">_)</a> <a id="13268" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13269" href="Data.Fin.Subset.Properties.html#15787" class="Function">∪-comm</a> <a id="13276" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="13278" class="Symbol">_)</a> <a id="13281" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#12404" class="Bound">Disjoint-⁅x⁆∪S-T</a><a id="13297" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="13302" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#13302" class="Function">Disjoint-S-T⇒∣S∪T|≡∣S∣+∣T∣</a> <a id="13329" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13331" href="Relation.Unary.html#3491" class="Function">Π[</a> <a id="13334" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#12142" class="Function">P</a> <a id="13336" href="Relation.Unary.html#3491" class="Function">]</a>
  <a id="13340" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#13302" class="Function">Disjoint-S-T⇒∣S∪T|≡∣S∣+∣T∣</a> <a id="13367" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13369" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#10761" class="Function">induction-on-elements</a> <a id="13391" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#12226" class="Function">P-∅</a> <a id="13395" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#12298" class="Function">inductive-step</a>
</pre>
We define isomorphisms of finite subsets:

<pre class="Agda"><a id="_≅_"></a><a id="13466" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#13466" class="Function Operator">_≅_</a> <a id="13470" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13472" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1064" class="Function">Subset</a> <a id="13479" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3410" class="Generalizable">m</a> <a id="13481" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13483" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1064" class="Function">Subset</a> <a id="13490" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3412" class="Generalizable">n</a> <a id="13492" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13494" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">Set</a> <a id="13498" class="Symbol">_</a>
<a id="13500" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#13500" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="13502" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#13466" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="13504" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#13504" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="13506" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13508" href="Data.Product.Base.html#852" class="Function">∃</a> <a id="13510" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13511" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1584" class="Function Operator">_∈</a> <a id="13514" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#13500" class="Bound">S</a><a id="13515" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13517" href="Function.Bundles.html#12701" class="Function Operator">↔</a> <a id="13519" href="Data.Product.Base.html#852" class="Function">∃</a> <a id="13521" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13522" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1584" class="Function Operator">_∈</a> <a id="13525" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#13504" class="Bound">T</a><a id="13526" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
`mk≅` is just a specialized version of `mk↔`, to help with type inference:

<pre class="Agda"><a id="mk≅"></a><a id="13617" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#13617" class="Function">mk≅</a> <a id="13621" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13623" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13624" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#13624" class="Bound">to</a> <a id="13627" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13629" href="Data.Product.Base.html#852" class="Function">∃</a> <a id="13631" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13632" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1584" class="Function Operator">_∈</a> <a id="13635" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3426" class="Generalizable">S</a><a id="13636" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13638" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13640" href="Data.Product.Base.html#852" class="Function">∃</a> <a id="13642" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13643" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1584" class="Function Operator">_∈</a> <a id="13646" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3428" class="Generalizable">T</a><a id="13647" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="13650" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13651" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#13651" class="Bound">from</a> <a id="13656" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13658" href="Data.Product.Base.html#852" class="Function">∃</a> <a id="13660" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13661" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1584" class="Function Operator">_∈</a> <a id="13664" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3428" class="Generalizable">T</a><a id="13665" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13667" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13669" href="Data.Product.Base.html#852" class="Function">∃</a> <a id="13671" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13672" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1584" class="Function Operator">_∈</a> <a id="13675" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3426" class="Generalizable">S</a><a id="13676" class="Symbol">)}</a>
  <a id="13681" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13683" href="Function.Definitions.html#1256" class="Function">Inverseᵇ</a> <a id="13692" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#150" class="Datatype Operator">_≡_</a> <a id="13696" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#150" class="Datatype Operator">_≡_</a> <a id="13700" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#13624" class="Bound">to</a> <a id="13703" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#13651" class="Bound">from</a>
  <a id="13710" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13712" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3426" class="Generalizable">S</a> <a id="13714" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#13466" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="13716" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3428" class="Generalizable">T</a>
<a id="13718" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#13617" class="Function">mk≅</a> <a id="13722" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13723" class="Argument">to</a> <a id="13726" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13728" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#13728" class="Bound">to</a><a id="13730" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="13732" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13733" class="Argument">from</a> <a id="13738" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13740" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#13740" class="Bound">from</a><a id="13744" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="13746" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13748" href="Function.Bundles.html#14548" class="Function">mk↔</a> <a id="13752" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13753" class="Argument">to</a> <a id="13756" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13758" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#13728" class="Bound">to</a><a id="13760" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="13762" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13763" class="Argument">from</a> <a id="13768" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13770" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#13740" class="Bound">from</a><a id="13774" class="Symbol">}</a>
</pre>
<pre class="Agda"><a id="≡-∃∈"></a><a id="13789" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#13789" class="Function">≡-∃∈</a> <a id="13794" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13796" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13797" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#13797" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="13799" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#13799" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="13801" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13803" href="Data.Product.Base.html#852" class="Function">∃</a> <a id="13805" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13806" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1584" class="Function Operator">_∈</a> <a id="13809" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#3426" class="Generalizable">S</a><a id="13810" class="Symbol">)}</a>

  <a id="14041" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#14041" class="Function">to₁-injective</a> <a id="14055" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14057" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14058" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#14058" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14060" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#14060" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="14062" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14064" href="Data.Product.Base.html#852" class="Function">∃</a> <a id="14066" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14067" href="Data.Fin.Subset.html#1584" class="Function Operator">_∈</a> <a id="14070" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#14006" class="Bound">S</a><a id="14071" class="Symbol">)}</a>

      <a id="14297" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#14297" class="Function">₁∘ι≡₁</a> <a id="14303" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14305" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#2226" class="Field Operator">_₁</a> <a id="14308" href="Function.Base.html#1115" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="14310" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#14235" class="Function">ι</a> <a id="14312" href="Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#1557" class="Function Operator">≗</a> <a id="14314" href="Causality.Data.Fin.Subset.html#2226" class="Field Operator">_₁</a>
